   10 # Normalization Test Suite
   11 # Format:
   12 #
   13 #   Columns (c1, c2,...) are separated by semicolons
   14 #   They have the following meaning:
   15 #      source; NFC; NFD; NFKC; NFKD
   16 #   Comments are indicated with hash marks
   17 #   Each of the columns may have one or more code points.
   18 #

   20 # 1. The following invariants must be true for all conformant implementations
